Anti-Japanese Iron Blood Corps

Someone Initiates the Formation in the City

Since the Japanese military's atrocities against our Northeast occurred, the whole country has been filled with grief and indignation. Resisting Japan and saving the country is what everyone desires. However, the atrocities did not happen overnight, so there must be a firm will and sustained effort to thwart the brutality of the Japanese and save our country from the brink of collapse. Recently, many people in the city have initiated the organization of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Ten-Person Corps. The declaration and articles of faith are as follows: Our declaration: The fierce and brutal Japanese imperialists have occupied our Northeast, robbed us of countless treasures, and massacred countless of our compatriots, and have not stopped even now. Even if it stops temporarily, it is difficult to guarantee that it will not happen again in the future. We do not want to be slaves of a conquered nation. We want to rise up and fight them to the death, not only to save the country, but also to save ourselves, to save our race. We have made up our minds, no more empty talk, no more half-heartedness, no more living in a drunken dream. We want to clench our teeth, be patient, realistic, and constantly follow our sacred articles of faith, and use the conscience and perseverance of each of our ten people to defeat the fierce and brutal Japanese imperialists who are oppressing us, robbing us, massacring us, wanting to destroy our country and exterminate our race. Our articles of faith are: (1) Do not buy Japanese goods; (2) Do not work for the Japanese; (3) Prepare for war against Japan (this article will be changed if you are in the military: rather die fighting the Japanese than surrender); (4) Promote the organization of the Ten-Person Corps. Our oath is: I solemnly swear that I will use my conscience and perseverance to implement our articles of faith: (1) Do not buy Japanese goods; (2) Do not work for the Japanese; (3) Prepare for war against Japan; (4) Promote the organization of the Ten-Person Corps. Never forget, never relax. If I violate this oath, I am willing to accept the most severe sanctions of this corps. Our hope is that, from the day the first Ten-Person Corps is established, each person will form a Ten-Person Corps within ten days, for a total of one hundred members. Then, within ten days, each person will form another Ten-Person Corps, for a total of one thousand members. From this promotion, the organization will grow tenfold and the members will grow tenfold every ten days. In less than three months, it will be widespread throughout the country. The first organization of the corps was solemnly established in the energetic morning light at 7 AM yesterday, with an old gentleman presiding over the oath-taking ceremony. The ceremony was extremely solemn and tragic. There is no leader, no burden, and no organization. The corps is actively developing the organization and plans to hold a joint gathering of one hundred people on National Day to discuss practical methods for resisting Japan and saving the country.

Department Stores Resolve to Eliminate Japanese Goods

The Association Will Send Personnel to Seal the Goods in Each Store

The Goods Inspection Committee Ordered Yesterday to Obey

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce's Japanese Goods Inspection Committee held its fifth regular meeting yesterday, attended by Qiu Liangyu, Pan Yisan, Ye Jiaxing, Shi Jiumao, Yu Yangzhou, Chen Guichu, Yuan Hongjun, etc., with Ye Jiaxing as chairman. The following cases were discussed: (1) The Chinese Alkali Industry Association sent a letter stating that non-Japanese goods, such as match stems and rosin, were detained at the Lida factory, requesting negotiation for their return. It was resolved to hand it over to the investigation team. (2) The Great China Match Company sent a letter requesting instructions on how to establish an inspection team, but the industry has not organized an association and is not a member of the Chamber of Commerce. It was resolved to reply that, since the industry has no trade association, it is not convenient to organize an inspection team according to the association's general rules. If any colleagues privately import Japanese goods, they can report them to the association or the Anti-Japanese Association as much as possible. (3) It was reported that Zhang Xingtao, chairman of the Hardware Industry Association, was sheltering Japanese goods, requesting sanctions. It was resolved: (1) To warn Zhang Xinghai; (2) To require the industry to organize an inspection team within three days of receiving the letter and report the organization situation for record; (3) To require the industry to seal all unregistered Japanese goods and Western goods sold by Japanese firms immediately. (4) The Department Store Industry Association sent a letter stating that it has decided on a method for eliminating Japanese goods, but it feels difficult to implement it in the three major companies, requesting assistance from personnel. It was resolved: (1) To reply to the industry association to quickly send personnel to seal the goods; (2) To send a letter to the three companies, stating that they must not refuse when the Department Store Industry Association comes to seal Japanese goods. (5) The Lighter and Gacha Industry Association sent a letter asking whether all items other than cotton seeds are prohibited from being sold to the Japanese, requesting a reply immediately. It was resolved that all items are prohibited, and a letter was sent to reply to the association. (6) The Blacksmith Industry Association sent a letter offering a method of contributing to the boycott of goods, requesting adoption. It was resolved to reply that it has been approved. (7) The Mercerized Cotton Weaving Industry Association sent a letter requesting clarification on three points. It was resolved: (A) Each team will formulate its own detailed rules for handling affairs within the team; (B) Inspectors will naturally receive rewards for finding Japanese goods. The reward method will be determined separately; (C) All factories in the industry can be inspected, but they must have a certificate. (8) The Steel and Tin Industry Inspection Team was named the "Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of the Copper and Tin Industry," which does not comply with the name stipulated in Article 2 of the general rules. Should it be corrected to show uniformity? It was resolved to reply to the association to correct the name to the Steel and Tin Industry Inspection Team. (9) Articles 10 and 11 of the general rules have provisions for rewards and punishments, but the regulations have not yet been formulated. Now, due to the tense anti-Japanese atmosphere, these regulations should be implemented urgently. Please decide on the drafting personnel and scope. It was resolved to appoint Qiu Liangyu, Pan Yisan, and Ye Jiaxing to draft the reward and punishment regulations. (10) It was reported that Zhu Chunbo, owner of the Zhenhua Lishi Umbrella Factory, colluded with Japanese merchants to privately import Japanese goods. How should he be handled? It was resolved to hand it over to the investigation team. (11) Representatives from the medicine, ginseng and bird's nest, cotton cloth, and mercerized cotton weaving industries requested that the Anti-Japanese Association be sent a letter requesting that the registered Japanese goods be investigated as soon as possible, and that a pass be issued for the investigated Japanese goods to alleviate the difficulties of merchants. It was resolved to forward it to the Anti-Japanese Association. (12) The Timber, Noodle Shop, and Grain Shop Associations sent a letter stating that they have established an inspection team, requesting filing for record. It was resolved to correct the filing for record.

Chairman Gong Jingyan. Resolutions: (1) From today onwards, all firms in the industry will swear never to import Japanese goods again. (2) The association's inspection team will be divided into ten districts, with each district divided into sections. Each section will elect several officers, and the officers will elect two chief officers. (3) Each day, members of the association's committee will lead the officers to work and inspect by district until the root is completely eliminated. (4) If the association's inspection finds that various firms have indeed imported and not sold a large amount of Japanese goods, they will be distributed to nine stalls at the original price until they are completely eliminated. (5) If any firm refuses inspection, they will be subject to the severe punishment stipulated by the association. (6) When the association's committee members and officers conduct inspections, they must carry the association's official letter and inspection certificate as proof. (7) If any firm violates the association's regulations and secretly hides Japanese goods, once discovered, it will be treated as secretly importing Japanese goods. (8) The association will hire four people every day to secretly and strictly inspect the purchase samples of various firms in the foreign firm street. Once discovered, it will be reported to the association and dealt with strictly according to the regulations without leniency. (9) The association will hire four bicycle teams every day to secretly inspect around the Japanese sugar warehouses on Chinese and foreign streets. Once discovered, it will be reported to the association and dealt with strictly according to the regulations and reported to the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association. (10) The association will organize a national salvation volunteer corps and publicly elect Lu Wenji and Cheng Wensheng as members to draft detailed rules and regulations. The association's entire staff must work hard from today onwards, and actively carry out inspections. Yesterday, Wei Shaolin, a Chinese from Canada, personally visited the office to meet with the overseas representatives, reporting that when the ship passed through Japan, he witnessed the miserable conditions suffered by the overseas Chinese, and requested that the representatives do their best to unite the nation to resist foreign aggression. The representatives were extremely inspired.

Fifth District 98

Patrol Officer Beaten by a Group of Assailants

Thirty-Odd People Holding Banners

Invaded the Station Shouting Slogans

Patrol Officer Liu Guoshu was Dragged Out

And Brutally Beaten Before They Scattered Without a Trace. The Baoshan Road Fifth District Public Security Bureau was suddenly attacked by dozens of people yesterday evening, and patrol officer Liu Guoshu was beaten and injured. According to the Public Security Bureau, the incident occurred at around 6:30 PM. More than 30 people suddenly came to the outside of the district station, holding banners in their hands. The leading persons, wearing suits, invaded the station, shouting words like "Down with You Bolu" and knocking hard on the table in the preliminary hearing office. At that time, Patrol Officer Liu Guoshu was in the patrol officer's room next to the preliminary hearing office. He went out to investigate after hearing the sound, but the comers grabbed Liu without asking any questions, dragged him out of the station, and beat him at the entrance of Tianjili. After the incident, they scattered without a trace. It was also heard that when the incident occurred, Public Security Bureau Director Chen was also in the station because he was inspecting in Zhabei and witnessed the incident. The patrol officer was severely beaten and injured. The pistol he was carrying and 17 bullets were taken away by the crowd. "A reactionary leaflet of the Declaration of the China Literature and Art Research Case Society" was also found. The injured Liu Guoshu was sent to Jisheng Hospital on Baoshan Road for treatment by the station. The head, waist, back and other parts were severely injured.

Party, Government, and Military Affairs 99

Inquiry into You Bolu and Others

Conflicting Statements from Chang Ching Police Witnesses

Another Deceased Identified as Cai Yongfang

Sixth District Party Headquarters Requests Severe Punishment

Regarding the incident of the Fifth District Public Security Bureau of Zhabei Baoshan Road police shooting civilians, Mayor Zhang sent representatives Yu Hongjun and others. After a detailed investigation the previous day, yesterday starting from 10:00 AM at the Municipal Government, Party Headquarters representative Wu Kaixian, Municipal Government representative Yu Hongjun, and Garrison Headquarters representative Jiang Yi, etc., interrogated You Bolu of the Fifth Public Security Bureau and other Chang Ching police, inquiring about the circumstances of the incident. They also summoned Sixth District Party Headquarters representative Yang Youren and related witnesses to inquire about everything. However, the statements from various Chang Ching police and related witnesses differed. The inquiry continued until around 2:00 PM, and as there were no results, they adjourned and decided to continue the inquiry today. After the three representatives completed their inquiry, they met with Mayor Zhang to report. In the afternoon, they revisited the Public Security Bureau to check on the detention of You and others.

Another Deceased Identified The Shanghai Packing Industry Workers' Union representative stated that the Fifth District Public Security Bureau Chief You Bolu brutally killed two compatriots. One was already claimed by family, but the other's name was unknown. It is now known that the deceased's name was Cai Yongfang, 22 years old, from Yuyao, Zhejiang. He worked as a bookbinder at Shiyongji Binding Shop in Xingyeli, Xibao Road. He was a member of the Shanghai Packing Industry Workers' Union. He had been suffering from an eye ailment for several days, and on the 1st of this month, at 8:00 PM, he went to a bathhouse at the south end of Qiujiang Road to bathe. After bathing, he returned to work and passed by the Fifth District Office. At that moment, District Chief You shouted for the police to open fire, and he was tragically killed by bullets. This person was usually honest and kind, and well-liked by his colleagues. He had worked at Shiyongji for many years. His family has now been notified. His father is a shop assistant in a rice store in his hometown. He was an only son, who married last September but has no children yet. Now he has met with this calamity.

Mother of Shen Wanlin Cries In the case of the Fifth District Police Station officers killing people, yesterday a woman named Shen Yan, mother of the deceased, filed a petition with the local court, stating that one of the deceased was her son, Shen Wanlin, 18 years old. He was already trying to avoid the area when the officers opened fire, resulting in him being shot in the back and dying. He was innocent and suffered an undeserved fate, and she requested justice. Prosecutor Yang opened a preliminary hearing. The woman stated that the police district chief and officers should be severely punished according to the law. The judge stated that District Chief You Bolu and six officers are currently being investigated by the Public Security Bureau, and after the case is handed over, it will be handled according to the law. The judge stated that her son's body has already been examined and she can claim it. The woman repeatedly requested justice, and the judge repeatedly consoled her before she left in tears.

Sixth District Party Headquarters' Petition The Sixth District Party Headquarters held a plenary meeting of district party members specifically for this matter and passed a resolution to petition, stating, "Petition regarding the Fifth District Chief You Bolu ordering the firing of guns and killing of innocent people, requesting that the petition be forwarded to the Supervisory Committee to expel You from his probationary party membership, and further request the municipal government to swiftly sentence You to capital punishment, confiscate his family property, and compensate the injured and deceased, to quell public anger and maintain party discipline. We have investigated that the current situation is extremely serious, and anti-Japanese sentiment is growing stronger. Therefore, the military and police responsible for local security, as well as patriotic individuals, should stand on the same front and demonstrate a spirit of cooperation in resisting aggression. This is a revolutionary understanding that should not be ignored. Unexpectedly, Fifth District Chief You Bolu, as a probationary party member and responsible for public security, should consider how to lead the public and work hard in the face of anti-Japanese national salvation, so as not to fail the central government's profound intentions for resisting Japan. However, the reality is the opposite, which pains us greatly. We will now briefly describe the circumstances (this paragraph has already been seen in yesterday's newspapers, the same as what was described by Yang Youren and Feng Xiancheng, members of the Sixth District Party Headquarters standing committee, so it is omitted). Based on the above facts, it is known that You Bolu's arrogance and violence are undeniable. The people gathered and refused to disperse, simply wanting to understand the outcome of the punishment of the offending police officers. Whether there were malicious individuals mixed in, we dare not say, but the people were all motivated by patriotic fervor, and even if they slightly overstepped the bounds of propriety, there was no reason to open fire and kill them. Moreover, according to eyewitnesses, the people did not rush into the Fifth District, nor did they take any action to fire first. Therefore, under such circumstances, the public security chief, no matter how violent, had no right to open fire freely. Furthermore, before the firing of guns, the district executive committee members, Tang and Yang, were still talking to him. If the situation was truly urgent, he should have consulted with them to seek a proper solution. In addition, the Fifth Railway Regiment fire brigade and other parties could have been called for assistance, but You did not heed this. Thus, relying solely on his own anger, he used the people as target practice. The pain of this matter is beyond measure. It has already been brought up at the forty-first executive committee meeting, and everyone believes that if this kind of matter is not severely punished, then the party's faith in the people will be completely lost. Therefore, the following resolutions were made: (1) Request that the Council forward the petition to the Supervisory Committee to expel You from his probationary party membership. (2) Request that the municipal government sentence You Bolu to capital punishment, confiscate his family property, and compensate the injured and deceased, etc. These matters are on file. We hereby list the facts and respectfully request your review and strict execution. We are awaiting your orders. Respectfully submitted."

You Bolu to be Sent to Court Yesterday, the reporter visited Public Security Bureau Chief Chen Xizeng to inquire about the handling of You Bolu's case. Chen replied that the case is currently being jointly investigated by the Party, government, and military to determine the truth. You Bolu is currently being held at the Public Security Headquarters and will be handed over to the court tomorrow for legal proceedings.

Litigation and Disaster Relief 101

Norwegian Merchant Sues for One Hundred Gold Pieces All Donated to Disaster Relief Agency The Yinheng Foreign Goods Firm previously violated a contract to purchase goods from a Norwegian merchant. The Norwegian merchant hired lawyer Lin Yingqing to file a lawsuit for damages with the First Special District Local Court, requesting that the defendant be ordered to compensate for losses of over 700 taels of silver. Yinheng argued that the violation was due to a breach of contract and filed a counterclaim, also requesting that the plaintiff be ordered to compensate for losses of over 800 taels of silver. Each side insisted on its own version of events. Yesterday morning, Judge Li Mo of the First Special Court summoned both parties for a hearing. After lawyer Lin Yingqing for the plaintiff explained the case, he stated that the plaintiff did not intend to keep the damages claimed for himself and was willing to donate the entire amount to Chinese flood relief. Judge Li praised the merchant's goodwill and advised both parties to reconcile. The defendant also complied with the judge's intention to settle the matter amicably and was willing to pay some compensation for the losses. As a result, the defendant compensated the plaintiff for 100 taels of silver in losses, which would be sent to the flood relief agency and donated in the plaintiff's name, with the receipt given to the plaintiff. Both parties had no objections to this settlement method and signed the settlement in court. Using the funds obtained from the lawsuit to generously assist in disaster relief is truly unprecedented. The charity of the Norwegian merchant is especially commendable.

The Kean Steamer Catches Fire in the Huangpu River 102

Significant Losses

Shipping Cargo to Xinghua The Kean steamer, which sails between Shanghai, Fuzhou, and Xinghua, is owned by the Ministry of the Navy and leased to shipping merchants to transport cargo between Shanghai and Fujian. This time, after arriving in Shanghai from Fujian, it stopped on the Huangpu River at the opposite side of the Ning Shao Steamer Company pier to load cargo, preparing to leave port today. While loading, a fire suddenly broke out in one of the cabins around 2:00 AM yesterday.

Carelessness in the Main Cabin Around 2:30 AM yesterday, the main cabin of the steamer had already loaded some of the flour, daylily, and fungus destined for Xinghua, etc., and the loading was not yet complete. Suddenly, a fire broke out in the main cabin. At the start of the fire, thick smoke billowed out from the cabin. The shipowner received the news and immediately ordered all the sailors on board to use pumps and hoses to spray water, but it was ineffective. The fire flared upwards.

Fireboats Assist in Fighting the Fire After the cargo in the cabin was burned by the fire, the crew and sailors were unable to extinguish it. They then notified the fire brigade for assistance. The Central Fire Brigade immediately dispatched a fireboat to the scene to assist in the firefighting. They vigorously sprayed water in the main cabin. By 7:30 AM, the fire had subsided somewhat, but smoke was still rising, so the firefighters remained on the ship to continue spraying water.

Clearing Damaged Cargo Besides the cargo in the main cabin that was destroyed by the fire, the cargo that was not affected by the fire was also soaked by water. The losses to passengers and cargo on board were already very significant. The steamer cannot leave port today and must clear the burned and water-soaked cargo. The families have already been notified. The ship's hull was not damaged, but the main cabin was damaged. Everything must be unloaded before a further inspection can be carried out.

China Industrial Bank 103

Panic Withdrawals Subside Yesterday

Japanese Shareholder Rumors Refuted

Recently, there were rumors fabricated by Japanese individuals regarding the China Industrial Bank, which led to a panic withdrawal of banknotes. Yesterday, after the bank entrusted various money shops to redeem banknotes on its behalf and the money shop guild published a notice to confirm this, the panic subsided. There were also rumors that it had Japanese shareholders and that due to anti-Japanese sentiments, the Japanese planned to withdraw their capital, leading to the turmoil. Yesterday, Lin Kanghou of the Bank Guild said that the bank is purely a Chinese merchant organization, and foreigners are not allowed to hold shares. Moreover, Article 7 of the bank's charter states that the government provides official shares, and commercial shares are raised by the commercial founders. This further proves that the rumors of Japanese shares are unfounded.

Second Lieutenant Li Yushu Wins First Place Overall

The Chinese detachment of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps held its 25th annual shooting competition at the Hongkou Shooting Range the other day, in order to train troops and expand shooting skills. Therefore, all participants were encouraged to be in good spirits and hone their skills to compete. Looking at the entire competition, the offensive style was the most exciting. Not only were the steps orderly and fast, but the loading and firing were also extremely rapid. The movements of lying prone and crouching in trenches, and then charging forward after opening fire on the ground, were particularly brave and sharp. Qi Shiying Returns to Shanghai Yesterday 105

Denies Representing Chairman Jiang to Japan His Trip Was Solely for Personal Matters Japanese newspapers in the city had previously reported that Mr. Qi Shiying's trip to Japan was to represent Commander-in-Chief Jiang in discussions with the Japanese government and public. Recent Situation of the Ministry of Transportation's International Radio Station 108

Our country's only channel for foreign communication is the Ministry of Transportation's International Radio Station. Since its establishment in the winter of last year, the station has adopted the latest system for internal arrangements, and the management is also quite effective. As a result, business is booming. It is said that the initial monthly revenue was only 30,000 to 40,000 yuan, but it has recently increased to about 200,000 yuan. This shows the trend of regaining control of our rights. During the recent invasion of the three eastern provinces by the brutal Japanese, all foreign propaganda and official telegrams were sent and received by this station, without relying on foreign companies. As for various official telegrams to Geneva, they were all sent by the Sino-French Radio Station of this station and relayed by Paris. On the day after the incident, all Japanese atrocities were spread throughout the city of Geneva. This shows the agility of the station's staff.

They rescued four children: A'kang, a seven-year-old from Ningbo; Xu Baohe, a ten-year-old; Wang Xinlin, a nine-year-old, both from Nanjing; and Shi Xiaoxizi, a fourteen-year-old from Zhenjiang. These individuals, along with the suspect Zhao Duanshi (from Anhui), were handed over to the First Special District Court for interrogation. This has been reported in this newspaper. A'kang, the child from Ningbo, has already been claimed by his father, Zhao A'fa. The remaining three children, including Xu Baohe, have been temporarily sent to the Women and Children's Relief Association for care, pending family recognition. The case has now concluded and is awaiting sentencing. Yesterday, Judge Xiao Xieffen from the Third Criminal Court sentenced Wang Huanan, Chen Xianren, and Chen Zhangshi to four years of imprisonment each, and Wang Lichun and Yang Wanchun to one year of imprisonment each. Before the final judgment, the number of days detained will be deducted at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. Zhao Duanshi was found not guilty and immediately released after Attorney Zhang of the police station declared that he would not appeal.

Opening Announcement of the Sino-American Department Store 114

The Sino-American Department Store, located east of the Xixin Bridge on Avenue Edward VII, was founded by Mr. Hu Mouzhou several years ago. It sells a full range of Chinese and Western goods at reasonable prices, and its business is very prosperous. Now, for the convenience of customers, a Sino-American Company has been established on the west side. It is grand in scale and rich in merchandise. Except for absolutely prohibited Japanese goods, it offers all famous Chinese and Western products, cosmetics, and more, all at low prices and high quality. Female staff are employed to provide attentive service. The grand opening will take place soon.

Exquisite Cuisine at the Hygienic Russian Restaurant 115

The Hygienic Russian Restaurant, located at No. 177 on the west side of Sichuan Road, Laobazi Road, Hongkou, opened last month. The head chef has served in the Russian army for several wars and is a renowned cook. All the chefs he employs are also trained by him. Therefore, the exquisite quality of the cuisine has already been praised by those who have tasted it. Furthermore, the cleanliness of the ingredients, the elegance of the furnishings, and the attentive service of the staff all adhere to the principles of hygiene. The prices range from eight dimes and five dimes to a la carte options. Coupon books are also available, priced at seven yuan and five yuan each, and can be used ten times.

Qian Jianqiu Practicing as a Lawyer 116

Joining Forces with Dr. Huang Biying to Establish a Law Firm

Ms. Qian Jianqiu, a Doctor of Law who studied in the United States, is the first Chinese female student to obtain this degree. Upon returning to China this summer, she immediately proceeded to obtain her lawyer's license and prepare for the establishment of her law firm. It is heard that Dr. Qian joined the Bar Association last month and has now joined forces with Dr. Huang Biying, who also holds a Doctor of Law degree from the United States, to establish a law firm at No. 71 Sichuan Road, 4th floor of the East Asia Bank. The interior design is quite complete, and they will officially open for business soon. Both Dr. Qian and Dr. Huang have profound legal knowledge and outstanding character, and it is expected that they will safeguard human rights.

Zhonghe Bank 117

No Relation to Zhonghe Bank of Chongqing

E Chen She states: The Shenzhuang of the Chongqing Zhonghe Bank, formerly located at No. 79 Zhonghe Lane, Sima Road, was a Shanghai branch of the Chongqing bank that was closed down last year under the orders of the head office. This spring, the Shanghai Zhonghe Commercial Savings Bank was established at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Pentang Lane, and has been in business for half a year. Recently, some people have mistakenly believed that this bank is related to the Chongqing Zhonghe Bank. In fact, this bank was organized by Shanghai's financial community and has no connection with the former Chongqing Zhonghe Bank.

Fourth Brigade of the Defense Corps Recruiting Volunteer Members 118

The Fourth Brigade of the Zhabei Xingjiaqiao Defense Corps has repeatedly received orders from the corps headquarters to expand its membership. However, there are still very few applicants. The original members have been earnestly trained by the brigade commander Xing Minyi and his officers. At a time when foreign aggression is increasing daily and the national situation is tense, it is imperative to rise up at the first sound of the rooster and promote military preparedness. The brigade intends to accommodate as many members as possible. Those who are willing to receive military training should quickly come to the brigade and apply in accordance with the regulations.

Boshan Baitu Coal Selling Well 119

Genuine Products to Resist Japanese Coal

The Zhongyuan Coal Company is deeply concerned that Japanese coal is flooding the Shanghai market, accounting for eighty or ninety percent of the coal supply and causing a large outflow of wealth. Therefore, it has developed coal in the Baituchun mining area of Boshan, Shandong Province, and established a branch office in Qingdao to transport coal to Shanghai, supplying the needs of factories and households in Shanghai and other provinces. The Baituchun coal is of excellent quality and has very little ash content. It is not only superior to Japanese coal, but also far surpasses the coal from Kailuan and other mines. As a result, major factories are competing to purchase it, and the sales volume is quite large. Currently, Japanese soldiers are using violence to invade our Eastern Provinces, and the calls to resist Japanese coal continue to rise. Due to the obstructed transportation on the Beijing-Ningbo Railway, the source of Kailuan coal is scarce and the price is soaring. In order to help resist Japanese goods and sympathize with users, the Zhongyuan Coal Company is maintaining the same coal price and is not increasing it. The office, formerly located on Jixiang Street, is no longer suitable for operations. Starting from the first of this month, it has moved to a new building at No. 40 Rongyang Lane, Pingwang Street, Fuzhou Road, and is actively working to expand its business and prepare for a thorough resistance to Japanese coal.

Opening of the Great Shanghai Rubber Factory, a Chinese-Owned Enterprise 120

Zhang Henian, Zhu Ziqian, Zhang Pingshan, Wu Youlu, and others have established the Great Shanghai Rubber Factory in Rihui Port, Shanghai, to manufacture various rubber products. Mr. Zhang has been studying rubber for decades, so his products, such as Great Shanghai, Yanshou, Lan, and Taiji brand galoshes, are of excellent quality. Orders from Shanghai and other cities are very crowded.

Veterinary Doctor from the Commercial Inspection Bureau Goes to Hangzhou to Treat Cattle Disease 121

The dairy cows of the Hangzhou West Lake Milk Company have contracted red water disease. Mr. Zhang Xiongfei, the manager of the company, came to Shanghai to contact the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau and request treatment. The bureau dispatched Cai Wuji, the deputy director and veterinary technical officer, and Cheng Shaohui, a technical officer, carrying the necessary medicines to Hangzhou for treatment. It is said that the company has more than two hundred dairy cows and specializes in producing Full Head condensed milk and other high-quality products, making it the most well-equipped condensed milk factory in our country.

Pushan Villa September Report 122

In September, Pushan Villa collected and buried unclaimed corpses in various parts of Zhabei, including twenty-one large coffins and two thousand and fifty-six small coffins. The Xieqiao branch buried two hundred and ninety small coffins. In addition, the public concession police stations and the Health Department sent a total of fifty-eight large coffins and two hundred and sixty-five small coffins of abandoned children and unclaimed corpses from hospitals within the concession for burial. Furthermore, the Water Disaster Relief Association commissioned the villa to handle the aftermath of the disaster victims. The villa collected and buried deceased disaster victims in the North and South City shelters, including fourteen large coffins and fifty-eight small coffins from the First Shelter on Liuying Road, Zhabei; twelve large coffins and twenty small coffins from the Chao Hui Villa in the South City; fifteen large coffins and one small coffin from the Shanghai Hospital; and two large coffins from the Zheshao Guild Hall and one large coffin from the Huzhou Wuyi Villa. In total, the villa collected and buried one hundred and twenty-three large coffins and two thousand seven hundred and ninety small coffins, and provided one hundred and eleven large coffins and one thousand and twenty-six small coffins. The Pushan Hospital on Xinmin Road provided medical consultations and medicines to a total of five thousand eight hundred and eighty-one patients.

Mr. Zheng Guobin's Message (Regarding Raising Funds for the Volunteer Army) 124

With the national crisis at hand and foreign aggression pressing, the people of the country have risen up to organize volunteer armies to fight to the death against the tyrannical Japanese. Their ambition is admirable. However, at the beginning of preparations, money is needed everywhere as a prerequisite issue, which is fundraising. This kind of huge number can never be achieved by the power of one or two people. It is necessary to seek help from the group. Last time, the Shanghai Boy Scouts raised donations along the way for the flood disaster for a period of three days, and the results were considerable. For this kind of patriotic act, I believe that the citizens of Shanghai will be more enthusiastic than for the flood disaster. Now I will contribute my humble opinion to your magazine. This amount will be designated as the Volunteer Army Fund, specifically for the purchase of military equipment, clothing, and other combat supplies, and must not be used for other purposes. Publicity: Publish a notice in various daily newspapers to announce to the citizens of Shanghai that, regardless of the amount, large or small, according to their ability, there is no time limit. Even a copper coin can be donated. Set up widely available bamboo tubes, like postal mailboxes, with extremely short and concise slogans and serial numbers. They should be sealed on the outside and placed at crowded intersections, large companies, firms, large hotels, restaurants, and other public places. Afterwards, every three days, the person in charge should collect them once. Invite representatives from all walks of life to the venue to open and inspect them together, and publish the total amount in the newspaper to show credibility.

(Reply) Will be published immediately.

Mr. Dai's Message (Discussing Joining the Volunteer Army) 125

Since the tyrannical Japanese forcibly occupied the Northeast, the loss of life and property in our country is truly incalculable. All patriotic citizens cannot but resent it. The number of people joining the National Salvation Volunteer Army initiated in this city has been even more enthusiastic in recent days. I am determined to enlist as well, but I have not yet informed my parents. If I keep it a secret without telling them, there will inevitably be obstruction later. If I send a letter to humbly seek their opinion (because they are in Ningbo), I am afraid that my wishes will not be fulfilled, and my current position may be affected. Because I work in a shop that resembles a prison, I cannot go out except for important matters. I implore you to reply to how to deal with the above two points. (Reply) Since joining the Volunteer Army has various difficulties and you are afraid of affecting your career, you might as well think of other ways to resist Japan besides joining the army. There are many ways. You can review the methods discussed in the communications published in this column in recent days, or it may be helpful for reference.

Mr. Xu Shou Xian's Message (Regarding the Japanese Infiltrating Anti-Japanese Venues) 126

Last night (October 10th) at 7 o'clock, when more than 600 students from our school were holding the founding meeting of the Youth Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association in the evening school of the YMCA, several Japanese people suddenly mixed in and sat among them, looking around suspiciously. After being questioned by the students, they were ordered to leave, because their speech was incoherent and they could be identified as Japanese at a glance. As for the others who were wearing Chinese clothes, when asked, they were speechless. At this time when the national crisis is imminent, the people of the country are loudly calling for self-salvation and national salvation. When we hold meetings and discussions, the Japanese are insidious and cunning, probing our strengths and weaknesses everywhere, and using a group of lackeys and national traitors to serve them. When our proposals are decided, they are already prepared. Therefore, in future meeting venues, we should pay more attention to inspection to prepare for any eventuality. I dare to ask that this matter be published in your newspaper so that our compatriots can pay attention.

(Reply) Very good. It will be published to alert all parties. Correction: In the reply to Monk Dianchan in the September 25th issue, "Chaozhou Reinvigoration Association of Esoteric Buddhism" was mistakenly printed as "Lake." Also, "Wei" in "Jiang Zaqiao's work" was mistakenly printed as "Zuo." All should be corrected.

Weather Report 128

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Yangtze River basin and coastal areas south of Ma'anshan Island will have cloudy skies with fog or drizzle. The winds over the Yellow Sea and East China Sea will be gentle and unstable. The weather off the coast of Annam will be bad. A hurricane in the Pacific Ocean was located near 17 degrees north latitude and 112 degrees east longitude around 6:00 PM and was moving extremely slowly. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in Shanghai was 75.4 degrees and the lowest was 61.7 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 71.5 degrees and the lowest was 44.6 degrees.

Education News Highlights

National Education Circles Hold 130

Memorial Rally for National Crisis

The Ministry of Education, believing that the national education sector should hold a memorial rally for the national crisis in response to Japanese atrocities, issued a circular to education departments and bureaus in various provinces and cities, as well as national and private colleges and universities. The document referenced Administrative Yuan Order No. 4954, which stated, "Approved in the Office of Civil Servants of the National Government Document No. 7986, it is stated that the Central Executive Committee's Special Letter No. 959 has decided that all schools should hold a memorial rally for the national crisis and observe three minutes of silence to express mourning. Additionally, lectures on the history of national humiliation and the course of the Japanese occupation of the three northeastern provinces should be given. It is hoped that the Ministry of Education will be ordered to direct all schools across the country to comply." In accordance with this directive, the original document was copied and sent for compliance. In addition to replying to the letter, the original copied document was sent for the Department to direct all schools under its jurisdiction to comply. This order, including the copied document, was issued. The military occupation of the Eastern Provinces by the Japanese army is truly a great humiliation for the country and should be urgently carried out to promote national spirit and jointly face the national crisis. Especially for young students, patriotic thoughts should be stimulated. The Committee has now decided that all schools should hold a memorial rally for the national crisis and observe three minutes of silence to express mourning. Additionally, lectures on the history of national humiliation and the course of the Japanese occupation of the three northeastern provinces should be given. This letter is specifically sent for you to order the Ministry of Education to direct all schools across the country to comply. To the National Government, Standing Committee members Chiang Kai-shek, Sun Ke, Ding Weifen, Hu Hanmin, Dai Chuanxian, Chen Guofu, Ye Chucang, Yu Youren, Zhu Peide, 20, 9, 26.

Jiangsu Education Department Orders 131

Educational Administrative Personnel Must Perform Their Duties

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education issued an order to its subordinates stating, "Since the Japanese army has ravaged and invaded our territory, the morale of soldiers and people's emotions are intense. The central government has clear instructions regarding the patriotic movement. All educational administrative personnel should, during this period of national crisis, demonstrate diligence and dedication. How to lead students, how to awaken the masses, so that the patriotic movement enters the right track, does not allow for any idleness, and is even more inappropriate to leave one's post without permission. Therefore, we hereby reveal the principles and clearly admonish that all staff members must comply. This order.

Zhejiang Education Department Promulgates Implementation Plan for Anti-Japanese National Salvation in Educational Institutions at All Levels Throughout Zhejiang Province (3) 132

(4) Administrative Aspects

Principals should develop a calendar of anti-Japanese national salvation teaching activities and proceed on a daily basis, so as to avoid any lack of planning. 1. Stipulate the central issue of daily training and notify teachers to implement it. 2. Stipulate the order of dates for gatherings of teachers and staff and the central points of discussion. 3. Stipulate the steps and methods for visiting households on a regular basis. 4. Stipulate the progress of teaching training and implement it in stages. 5. Stipulate the number of children's gatherings and their talking points. 6. Stipulate the methods for checking children's health and the steps for carrying them out. 7. Create tests to measure the results of implementation. 8. Regularly contact other schools to carry out positive and concrete measures together. 9. Review all anti-Japanese national salvation teaching materials. 10. Stipulate other emergency steps and prepare in advance on a regular basis.

(D) Social Education Institutions

1. People's education centers at all levels should post the news from wireless broadcasts daily, (1) using clear writing and posting it in thoroughfares, (2) notify or print and distribute to educational institutions at all levels by telephone, and publicize and promote it at the same time. 2. People's education centers at all levels should draft an outline of anti-Japanese national salvation propaganda and distribute it to educational institutions at all levels for joint propaganda. 3. People's education centers at all levels should compile and print propaganda materials, which should be jointly performed by all educational institutions and entertainment venues, in addition to performing them themselves. 4. People's education centers at all levels should draw or print propaganda drawings or pictorials and post them as much as possible. 5. People's education centers at all levels should individually or jointly appoint staff from rural and township education institutions or other personnel as temporary specially-contracted speakers to conduct organized propaganda. 6. People's education centers at all levels should, to the best of their ability, hold anti-Japanese exhibitions alone or in conjunction. 7. People's education centers and libraries at all levels should collect and supply materials on Sino-Japanese issues as much as possible. 8. Social education institutions at all levels may, at their discretion, suspend other activities and hold various anti-Japanese national salvation activities as much as possible. 9. Social education institutions at all levels should link with all sectors to organize various self-defense national organizations for general mobilization training, such as (1) organizing a self-defense group for a certain industry based on occupational groups, (2) organizing a self-defense group for a certain village based on village and neighborhood, (3) organizing a youth self-defense group based on age differences, etc., (4) organizing a women's nursing group, etc., based on gender differences. (Note) When organizing the above groups, it is necessary to first publicize the prevention of local security and take the opportunity to arouse the spirit of hatred towards the enemy. 10. Social education institutions at all levels in counties and cities should use public places to invite relevant personnel or personnel from their own institutions to hold public lectures. 11. Social education institutions at all levels should convene storytellers, provide them with anti-Japanese national salvation propaganda materials, and urge them to promote them together. 12. People's schools at all levels should make as many facilities as possible for anti-Japanese national salvation, and hold ten minutes of group exercises every day. (13) Reading rooms at all levels should post the Japanese newspapers first, add red circles to important news, and select important excerpts to post on nearby main roads. (End)

Order from the Jiangsu Education Department to Issue Measures for Resisting Japan and Saving the Nation 133

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education issued an order to the County Education Bureaus, stating: "The Japanese military's dispatch of troops to the Northeast, occupying our territory, and killing our officials and civilians is truly a great national humiliation. All young students in our primary and secondary schools who witness this situation should endure humiliation and contain their anger, working together with one heart to devise strategies for wiping out this disgrace and saving the nation. Regarding the methods for this national salvation movement, in addition to actively proceeding in accordance with the 'Education Guidelines for Volunteer Soldiers' promulgated by the Central Executive Committee and the 'Key Points for Guiding Student National Salvation Movements in Various Provinces and Cities' issued by the Ministry of Education, we are now, to unify objectives and achieve practical results, specially formulating the 'Implementation Measures for the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement in Secondary and Higher Education Institutions in Jiangsu Province' and the 'Implementation Measures for the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement in Primary Schools in Jiangsu Province,' and issuing them for implementation. In addition to separate orders, we are immediately forwarding the aforementioned two sets of measures for your bureau chief to follow and instruct your subordinates to follow as well. You must also submit detailed implementation plans for our records. This order includes two sets of measures."

Implementation Measures for the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement in Secondary and Higher Education Institutions in Jiangsu Province 134

Now, to facilitate the guidance of young students in this province in their national salvation movement and to enhance the efficiency of implementation, based on the Central Government's intentions and decrees, and the "Key Points for Guiding Student National Salvation Movements in Various Provinces and Cities" promulgated by the Ministry of Education, the "Implementation Measures for the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement in Secondary and Higher Education Institutions in Jiangsu Province" are formulated as follows:

1. Research, divided into courses, lectures, and books, etc. A. Regarding courses, materials related to the Sino-Japanese problem should be fully incorporated into the following subjects to enhance teaching efficiency: (1) History, (2) Geography, (3) National Language, (4) Politics, (5) Economics, (6) Foreign Languages (take Sino-Japanese relations dissertations as material). B. Regarding lectures, school faculty or invited celebrities should give regular lectures on the following topics: (1) History of Japanese Aggression Against China, (2) Japanese Policy of Aggression in Manchuria, (3) Research and Analysis of Japanese Political Parties, (4) Sino-Japanese Trade Issues, (5) The Pacific Issue, (6) Methods for Economic Severance with Japan, etc. C. Regarding books, more books and maps related to Sino-Japanese issues should be purchased and prepared for joint research by faculty and students.

2. Propaganda. When students organize lecture teams in their spare time, faculty members should be responsible for guiding them, paying special attention to the following points during lectures: (1) The purpose of Japanese provocations, (2) Japanese-occupied areas, (3) Destruction of important institutions in occupied areas, (4) Japanese acts of theft, (5) Japanese brutal acts in occupied areas, etc., (6) Permanent boycott of Japanese goods.

3. Training. (1) For high school and higher students: A. Organize volunteer soldiers in accordance with the Central Student Volunteer Soldier Measures. B. Intensify military training, paying special attention to sanitation. (2) For junior high school students: Intensify Boy Scout training. 4. Scope: All activities leading students in the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement shall comply with the regulations of the Central Government.

Implementation Measures for the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement in Primary Schools in Jiangsu Province 135

1. Objective: Based on the educational principles of the Three Principles of the People, and with Japan as the target, train children so that they have a deep understanding and memory of the historical humiliations inflicted on our country by Japanese imperialism. One method focuses on physical training and sincere inspiration, in order to cultivate healthy, patriotic youth to seek revenge and save the nation.

2. Methods: Abandon all empty talk and general discussions, adopt the principle of active implementation, and divide into three aspects: teaching, training, and administration. (1) Teaching: All teaching spirit should focus on the Anti-Japanese National Salvation issue, and the atrocities and aggressive policies of Japan against us in the past should be incorporated into the teaching materials of each subject as much as possible, taking the recent dispatch of troops to the Northeast as a starting point and proceeding in conjunction with each subject at the same time. For example, using the "Project-Based Learning Method," "Anti-Japanese National Salvation" can be used as the central unit for each subject's teaching design. In addition to teaching materials, collect and compile children's reading materials related to Japanese research and the history of national humiliation as much as possible, so that they can be inspired at all times to resolve to resist Japan and save the nation, without forgetting it over time. The physical education and hygiene subjects should pay more attention to methods of physical fitness and intensify training so that everyone has a healthy physique. (2) Training: With teachers as leaders, all teachers and students should take advantage of opportunities at any time and place, such as memorial weeks and morning meetings, to intensify training or encourage each other to implement the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement, and to ensure that their thoughts and actions are effectively put on the right track, such as adopting national goods, saving money to save the country, developing habits of hard work and endurance, and promoting healthy and strong physical exercises, etc. Anti-Japanese National Salvation maxims can also be formulated as armbands to be observed forever. On the one hand, arrange the environment with paintings, wall newspapers, slogans, etc., so that there are startling and alarming alerts everywhere. In addition, various competitions and propaganda that can stimulate their patriotic enthusiasm without hindering their studies should also be held from time to time. Outside of class, teachers should take advantage of the opportunity to guide them in various national salvation activities, such as adapting the recent Japanese atrocities into children's songs and scripts for them to perform, etc., in order to deepen their memory. (3) Administration: All faculty and staff should form an Anti-Japanese National Salvation Research Association to discuss all issues related to Anti-Japanese National Salvation, and to stipulate concrete implementation methods and the progress steps of teaching and training. At the same time, it is necessary to plan and promote the implementation of the cause so that it extends from the school to the nearby community, and should also enlighten students' families with the concept of Anti-Japanese National Salvation at any time, and conduct national salvation actions together. After the implementation of the school's Anti-Japanese National Salvation methods, the results obtained should be compiled into a report and submitted to the competent authority separately, and as a basis for pre-planning the second step of methods.

3. Precautions: When implementing the above methods, the following provisions should be strictly observed: (1) All actions should comply with the regulations of the Central Government and should be considered from a positive perspective. (2) Abandon empty talk and reckless action, and strive to be practical and effective. (3) Teachers should lead by example and be leaders of the children. (4) Teaching and guidance should be adapted to the needs of children's physical and mental health at all times, with the overall goal of achieving practical results quickly. (5) The attitude of principals, teachers, etc. should be extremely loyal and sincere so that children will always believe in them. (6) Focus on enabling automatic action, and avoid passive or compulsory behavior.

4. Supplementary Provisions: When these measures are implemented, each school may make changes according to the environmental conditions, but it should not violate the principles of the first objective. Local.

Private Elementary School Teachers Establish National Salvation Association 136

Private elementary school teachers in this city, initiated by Jingwen, Puzhi, Huiqun Girls' Middle School Attached Elementary School, and other schools, have formed the Shanghai Private Elementary School Anti-Japanese National Salvation Federation, and many have joined. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, the first executive committee meeting was held at the Qixing Seven Counties Association. Representatives from over twenty schools, including Chengzhong Attached Elementary School and Huiqun Girls' Middle School Attached Elementary School, attended. Cheng Zuxin and Wu Xiliang from Huiqun Girls' Middle School Attached Elementary School presided, and Ren Chengming recorded. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Economic severance with Japan. (2) Request the Ministry of Education to add military courses to elementary schools. The Changwus were elected as Huiqun Girls' Middle School Attached Elementary School, Puzhi, and Peiming Girls' Middle School Attached Elementary School. Chengzhong Attached Elementary School was appointed as the Publicity Officer, Shiran was appointed as the Organization Officer, and Puzhi was appointed as the Chief of General Affairs. It has been decided that McLean Road Peiming Girls' Middle School Attached Elementary School will be the general office, and Tilanqiao Huiqun Girls' Middle School Attached Elementary School, Dadongmen Shiran Elementary School will be the branch offices.

Jinan University Student Army Reorganized into Volunteer Army 137

President Zheng Hongnian Serves as Commander-in-Chief

National Jinan University is renowned for its students' robust physique and outstanding athletic performance, and it has always placed great emphasis on military training. In light of the recent incident in the Eastern Provinces, students are outraged by Japan's tyrannical behavior and have been unusually active in the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement. The student army has been expanded and reorganized into an all-student volunteer army, with intensified training. The university affairs meeting has resolved that President Zheng will serve as the Commander-in-Chief of the Student Volunteer Army, and the Commander-in-Chief has appointed military instructors Zhou Jiashou and Wang Xueyuan as Deputy Commanders, responsible for training. Peng Qinghe is the Chief of the General Corps, Cai Rongrui is the Commander of the First Battalion, Zhou Zhaoqin is the Commander of the Second Battalion, Huang Yulang is the Commander of the Third Battalion, Huang Weinan is the Commander of the Medical Team, Huang Yuru is the Commander of the Nursing Team, and Ye Yusheng is the Deputy Commander of the Nursing Team. The Commanders of each Company and Platoon will be appointed upon the recommendation of the Chief of the General Corps. Teaching martial arts is for killing the enemy. Additionally, faculty and staff at the university have also established a cadre study class, and three-fifths of the faculty and staff have volunteered to enlist and undergo rigorous training.

Amidst the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement 138

The Grandeur of Wang Jiyuan's European Painting Exhibition

The renowned painter Mr. Wang Jiyuan is holding an exhibition of his European works at the Mingfu Library of the Chinese Science Society at 533 Albert Road from October 1st to 10th. It has been open for several days, and crowds of viewers have been flocking to it every day, especially young students from various specialized schools. Being able to strive for academic research amidst the Anti-Japanese cries is truly the foundation of national salvation. According to Mr. Wang, during his travels in Europe, he witnessed the Japanese Art Association's international propaganda, which revealed its long-held ambition to dominate East Asia, causing Westerners to only know about Japan when talking about modern Eastern culture, without knowing about China. This is truly infuriating. He hopes that the domestic art world will unite and fight the tyrannical Japanese together, engaging in forceful propaganda internationally to wash away this shame. Students who have studied Western painting in Japan and have now returned to the country out of anger should continue their research in domestic art groups. Art is an endless pursuit for life, and it is the most important point in the survival of any nation. Mr. Wang's unwavering holding of the European painting exhibition in Shanghai, which is related to the views of various countries, during this national crisis shows the undying spirit of the new Chinese nation. As we try to read Mr. Wang's works, such as "Victory Gentleman," the atmosphere of innovation is filled in each painting. Whether it is oil painting or watercolor painting, they all have unique oriental style. There are two newly published collections on the venue, and the printing is also exquisite. It is said that there are still seven days of the exhibition.

My friend Zhu Ying took a letter he wrote to congratulate DY on his suicide to me a few days ago. In the letter are words, tears, and blood. How can I tell them apart? He even makes it so that those who don't plant rice eat good food, and those who plant rice don't have food to eat! Those who don't plant cotton wear good clothes, and those who plant cotton don't have clothes to wear! Those who don't build forests live in good houses, and those who build forests don't have houses to live in! People in this kind of empty and contradictory society are so distressed! Under these circumstances, most young people with weak will often become its victims! I often thought of committing suicide, and often ran to the Hexi Bridge or Guhong Bridge, twenty miles away from home, to commit suicide at night.

Since September 19th, the violent Japanese occupied our Eastern Provinces and massacred our people. The people of the country were unanimously indignant. The upper class's clothes The upper class is not limited by money, and wears silk and billie ni rong. (According to the authentic billie ni rong, it is a Western product.) However, the lining used is still inseparable from Japanese goods, such as rayon, sub-silk, and beautiful but not durable banling and so on. They are everywhere.

The middle and lower classes' clothes People in the middle and lower classes often use rushed billies, rushed tribute, etc. due to money relations, because silk, billie ni rong, etc. are expensive, and there are few beautiful domestic fabrics. (According to the rushed goods, they are all Japanese goods.) All middle and lower class people buy them because they are cheap and have an appearance. How much money is spilled out every year?

The history of domestic native cloth Domestic native cloth has a history of thousands of years. In this era of commercial warfare, it is not eliminated. It can maintain its inherent position. (Try to watch tenant farmers still wearing native cloth) Of course, there are considerable benefits. Its quality is strong. It is far better than Western goods, which are real billies, let alone Eastern goods. Its value is dozens of times cheaper than Western goods. For thousands of years, cold and heat have been used as clothes, so why not still use local cloth to make clothes now? Individuals save money and spill less money. Why not do it?

Blood-Tearful Words Amidst National Crisis 151

— Lü Bing

The Wokou (Japanese) have resorted to arms, violently occupying our land and cruelly slaughtering our compatriots. My friend Mr. Zhang studied in Japan several years ago. After arriving in Tokyo, he sought a moderate inn near the local provincial association, intending to move there. The innkeeper inquired about his name, nationality, and age. Immediately, he revealed a look of contempt and said, "The upper floors of our inn are for Japanese, the middle floors are for Koreans, and you, as a Chinese, can only live on the lower floors." From this, one can see that the Japanese regard us as even inferior to Koreans. What is bearable if this is not? The famous actor Gao Fu'an, once renowned both north and south, was celebrated wherever he went. Gao specialized in martial roles and was skilled in combat. One year, he traveled on the South Manchurian Railway from Dalian to Fengtian. The South Manchurian Railway was within the sphere of influence of the tyrannical Japanese, and unequal treatment often occurred between Chinese and Japanese. At that time, a Chinese woman with a young child was in the same carriage as Gao. The child, being ignorant, accidentally defecated due to diarrhea. This was seen by the Japanese in the adjacent seats, who all began to scold her noisily. The woman quickly got up to clean it, but the Japanese anger did not subside. They claimed that it harmed public hygiene and demanded that she be punished by licking up all the fecal matter. Gao, hearing this, felt indignation and stood up to argue with composure. Three or four Japanese, overpowered by reason, attempted to attack him. Gao knocked them all down. Knowing that he would be humiliated by the police upon arrival at the station, he escaped mid-journey by jumping out of the window. Afterward, the Fengtian consulate negotiated with our country's authorities. Gao was eventually arrested and imprisoned for several years. This incident was narrated by Mr. Liu and is also recorded in a certain factual novel. Even before our country is subjugated, the unreasonableness of the Japanese is already like this. From the small, one can see the large. It is needless to say that the three northeastern provinces have been ravaged and devastated this time. As fellow citizens of China, how can we constantly embrace a policy of non-resistance and allow their iron heel to spread?

Talk Section: Rotary Club

The Pestle of Knocking Dreams (4) 155

— Cheng Zhanlu

"Layman should know the difference between flowing with and against the current. This old monk has a clear explanation. Turning the chair in the direction of the Earth's rotation is called flowing with the current. It's just that the speed of the revolving chair is thousands of times faster than the Earth's rotation. Therefore, the world that the people on Earth have not yet encountered is already known to the person sitting on the revolving chair. Layman does not want to see that future golden world, but only wants to make that China of one or two hundred years ago appear before your eyes. This is also very easy. This old monk uses a method of flowing against the current, turning the revolving chair in the opposite direction of the Earth's rotation, which is called flowing against the current. It's just that the speed of the revolving chair is thousands of times faster than the Earth's rotation. For example, when walking, the person on Earth takes one step, but the person on the revolving chair has already retreated thousands of steps. Therefore, the world that has become history is not visible to the people on Earth. The person on the revolving chair only needs to keep reversing, and even the Han and Tang dynasties can be chased back, and one can personally witness their glory. How much more so is it to reverse the time of China one or two hundred years ago? This is how it is explained. "May I ask the old monk, how is it explained when time does not flow?"

"Layman, flowing with the current is the future view; flowing against the current is the past view... not flowing... is the present view."

"How is it called the present view?"

"This is also the wonderful use of the revolving chair. It does not make it flow with the current, nor does it make it flow against the current. Sitting on this chair, no matter how long you sit, it is still the present. Looking back at the people in the world, the young grow old, and the old die; only the person sitting on the revolving chair does not change in youth, does not change in complexion, and is always in the present state. This is called the non-flowing of time."

The settlement price of US currency was implemented yesterday, rising sharply by about five taels. The specie price rose slightly yesterday, and the situation was moderate. Book Review

Japan's Overseas Aggression and Overseas Chinese 172

By Shen Meizhen

At this moment, the brave soldiers in the Northeast are throwing their heads and spilling their blood, fighting heroically and indignantly against the artillery fire from the Japanese devils, who harbor sinister intentions. The book "Japan's Overseas Aggression and Overseas Chinese," compiled by my old friend Liu Shimu, has also been published. Reading this kind of book, which exposes the enemy's secret aggression, would already be heartbreaking in peacetime. Reading it now, when the nation is in peril, is even more infuriating. The Japanese are invading everywhere, flaunting their relatively strong national power, recklessly barging in, and not hesitating to become the world's criminal. It is hateful to think about it. However, hating them is also futile. Japanese artillery fire has already erupted uncontrollably in the Northeast, proving that their northern expansion policy has reached the boiling point. In this book, there is an explanation of their means of aggression: "Japan's means of aggression in the East are divided into two routes. One route is to use countless soldiers in northern China to expand their gradual and encroaching colonial policy, known as the Northern Expansion Faction. The other route is to use countless sailors in southern China to expand their all-encompassing colonial policy, known as the Southern Expansion Faction."

At this time, when their northern expansion is extremely active, it seems gratifying to expose the situation of their southern expansion.

Japanese imperialism's southern invasion has been carefully planned for more than just a day. It is only because the time is not yet ripe that it has not yet developed into the tragedy that the Northeast has suffered this time. We only see batches of advance invaders being sent to Southeast Asia. The amount of their investment in Southeast Asia is increasing year by year. At the same time, books advocating southern invasion and various practical activities related to preparing for southern invasion are also shifting from calm to complex. Therefore, those who are pessimistic about the world are paying close attention, fearing that Southeast Asia will be the fuse for a world war. This kind of worry, when compared to the beastly behavior that the Japanese are unleashing in the Northeast this time, is not unfounded. In this book, we can also find statements that are sufficient to cause this serious situation, such as "Southeast Asia, the world's richest resource, is naturally connected to Japan. With seasonal winds, a single sail can cross south, the sea waves do not rise, and the other shore of Southeast Asia can be reached. Southeast Asia is the former hometown of the Yamato people and today's new stage." From these few words, we can see what Southeast Asia is like in their minds.
